Grid is a program which makes it easy to add a gridded overlay onto an image. In other words, it squares up the image for you.\r\n\r\nSplitting an image up into sections, to help us draw it, is something humans have been doing for centuries. With the dawn of the twenty-first century, though, it seems we have let this technique stagnate. We are still drawing the grid by hand and that includes computers (line or pen tool anyone?). I am sure you agree when I say it is a good thing to teach children how to do by hand in their art class. But... it becomes tedious the more you do it and, once you know how to do it, there is very little to learn or improve upon. This is where Paint Grid comes in.\r\n\r\nTo use Paint Grid, drag and drop a .jpg or .png file into the preview area. Use the control panel on the right to adjust the amount of rows and columns you want. After that, set the thickness of the grid lines and its colour and when you are ready, click \"Save As\". From there, you can either print it or open it in your go-to painting/drawing application.\r\n\r\nBy using Paint Grid, you are reducing a task which can take tens of minutes (sometimes over an hour) to mere seconds. The credit freeze locks the data at the consumer reporting agency until an individual gives permission for the release of the data.\r\n\r\n# Lesson 4: Acquiring and understanding credit reports and credit scores - Consumers can typically check their credit history by requesting credit reports from credit agencies and demanding correction of information if necessary.\r\nIn the US, the Fair Credit Reporting Act governs businesses that compile credit reports. These businesses range from the big three credit reporting agencies, Experian, Equifax, TransUnion, to specialty credit reporting agencies that cater to specific clients including payday lenders, utility companies, casinos, landlords, medical service providers, and employers. The consumer credit reporting agencies it governs provide a free copy of the credit reports for any consumer who requests it, once per year.\r\n\r\n# Lesson 5: free credit monitoring and credit tracker - Credit report monitoring or credit tracking is the monitoring of one‚Äôs credit history in order to detect any suspicious activity or changes. Companies offer such service on a subscription basis, typically granting regular access to one‚Äôs credit history, alerts of critical changes to one‚Äôs credit history, and additional services. Credit monitoring can help detect credit related fraud and identity theft.\r\n\r\n# Lesson 6: fix your credit score ‚Äì credit repair - Credit score is calculated also by taking into account your history, but there are few things that you can do to create a real impact on your credit score.
